<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:специальность.html>специа́льность</a> (4096)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специальный.html>специа́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">speciálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специальность.html>специа́льность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">speciálʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специальность.html>специа́льности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специальность.html>специа́льности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специальность.html>специа́льностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>specialty, trade, profession <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">that in which one specializes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fail, come a cropper</li></ol>

***спешить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спешить.html>спеши́ть</a> (1190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">спѣшити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spěšiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*spěšiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hurry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*spěxъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">haste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*spěti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to advance, ripen, hurry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-xъ</i>. Equivalently from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">спех</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spex</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spetʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спешить.html>спеши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spešítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заспешить.html>заспеши́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспешить.html>поспеши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hurry, to hasten, to make haste, to be in a hurry</li>
<li>to be fast <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">said of clocks, watches</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства_2"></span></h3>

<p><b>спе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>ши́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный, <a href = vnd.unilang:безличный.html>безли́чный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <span>приставочные <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́па</a></span> заспешиться, поспешиться.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-спеш-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спешный.html>спе́шный</a> (20635)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***спина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спина́</a> (303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*spey-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sharp point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spine</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spike</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нка</a> (3332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спина́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spiná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спина́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spiná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>back <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a chair, couch or other furniture, of a dress or a shirt, of a tool, of an animal, or as a cut of meat</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>; headboard; backrest</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спираль.html>спира́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spirálʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спиральный.html>спира́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spirálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)спира́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)спира́льней</b>)
</p>

<li>helical</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a> (2816)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spirit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spīritus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spirt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спи́рта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>alcohol, spirits
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:технический.html>техни́ческий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">texníčeskij <b>spirt</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">denatured alcohol</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гидро́лизный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gidróliznyj <b>spirt</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cellulosic ethanol</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спиртной.html>спиртно́й</a> (6795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spirt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спиртной.html>спиртно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spirtnój</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>alcoholic, spirituous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спиртной.html>спиртно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:напиток.html>напи́ток</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spirtnój</b> napítok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">liquor</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>alcoholic</b> beverage</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:списать.html>списа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:списывать.html>спи́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to copy <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">writings</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to plagiarize <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">writings</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to write off

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:списать.html>списа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ненадобность.html>нена́добностью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spisátʹ</b> za nenádobnostʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to discard</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:списать.html>списа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>корабля́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spisátʹ</b> s korabljá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to transfer/post from a ship</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:список.html>спи́сок</a> (1365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pis-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to write</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>  + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">an object that remains after process is done</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:список.html>спи́сок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spísok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:список.html>спи́ска</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:список.html>спи́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:список.html>спи́сков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>list, register, roll <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">register or roll of paper consisting of an enumeration or compilation of a set of possible items</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вычеркивать.html>вычёркивать</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:вычеркнуть.html>вы́черкнуть</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:список.html>спи́ска</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vyčorkivatʹ/výčerknutʹ kovó-libo iz <b>spíska</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike someone off the list</span></div></dd></dl></li>
